  * grade_story_102.txt (grade=8.2)
    The map projection room provides a visually striking and thematically resonant setting that enhances the story's focus on "uncharted horizons." The amber light and cartographic imagery create an atmospheric backdrop that blends mystery and possibility. The timeframe—"during the hush after the wind no longer howls"—is elegantly woven into the plot's mechanics, making the setting essential rather than decorative. The sensory details effectively immerse readers in this liminal space between worlds.
